> Modular Frame (10/min)
  # Alternate: Bolted Frame:
    | Input/Output and Step Efficiency Values:
        - 15 Reinforced Iron Plate(s)
        - 280 Screws(s)
        - 15 MW(s)
        * 1 Assembler(s)
        * 150 m^2(s) (about 3 foundations minus belt space)
        * 2 steps into the chain from the top.
        ++ 10 Modular Frame per minute
    |- Reinforced Iron Plate (15/min)
